# E2R Stock-Web Historical Calibration / Sector-Archetype Residual Research Round

## 0. Research Metadata

```text
research_session = post_calibrated_sector_archetype_residual_research
mode = historical_trigger_level_calibration_after_stock_web_ohlc_breakthrough_v12
output_format = one_standalone_markdown_file

stock_agent_code_access_allowed = false
stock_agent_code_patch_allowed = false
stock_agent_live_scan_allowed = false
current_stock_discovery_allowed = false
production_scoring_changed = false
shadow_weight_only = true
handoff_prompt_embedded = true
handoff_prompt_executed_now = false

scheduled_round = R13
scheduled_loop = 11
completed_round = R13
completed_loop = 11
computed_next_round = R1
computed_next_loop = 12
round_schedule_status = valid
round_sector_consistency = pass

large_sector_id = L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC
canonical_archetype_id = R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM
fine_archetype_id = CROSS_ARCHETYPE_LOOP11_HIGH_MAE_4B_4C_GUARDRAIL
output_file = e2r_stock_web_v12_residual_round_R13_loop_11_L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC_R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM_research.md
price_source = Songdaiki/stock-web
stock_web_manifest_max_date = 2026-02-20
```

This loop adds **12** R13 cross-pattern independent cases, **8** counterexamples, and **12** residual errors for **R13 / L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC / R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM**.

R13 is the checkpoint round. It is not another sector room; it is the alarm panel that checks whether smoke from very different rooms is coming from the same wiring fault. The loop 11 source files created sector/canonical shadows. This R13 file asks whether the same residual keeps appearing across those shadows: high-MAE false positives, price-only Green, local 4B confusion, hard 4C lateness, and the opposite risk of over-penalizing clean structural positives.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

```text
current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy
previous_baseline_reference = e2r_2_0_baseline_reference
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = +2.0
stage3_yellow_total_min = 75.0
stage3_green_total_min = 87.0
stage3_green_revision_min = 55.0
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = +1.5
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = true
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = true
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = true
```

This R13 file does **not** re-propose these global axes as if they were new. It stress-tests them after loop 11. The new residual candidate is cross-archetype: **a strong price move or headline can remain a useful watch signal, but positive-stage promotion needs a non-price evidence bridge, and 4B/4C must be split into local price-only watch, full non-price risk overlay, and thesis-break route.**

## 2. Round / Large Sector / Canonical Archetype Scope

```text
scheduled_round = R13
scheduled_loop = 11
allowed_large_sector_id = L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC only
selected_canonical_scope = R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM
round_sector_consistency = pass
```

R13 uses the special cross-archetype canonical scope. It does not write `R13_L5_C20` or `R13_L6_C21`; those belong to R5/R6. The selected source rows intentionally span R1~R12 loop 11 so the failure mode is not mistaken for a single-sector artifact.

## 3. Previous Coverage / Duplicate Avoidance Check

Local loop 11 files show R1 through R12 complete. The immediately preceding R12 file points to R13 / loop 11. Therefore the scheduled state is valid.

Duplicate policy:

```text
same symbol + same trigger date + same evidence family is not re-promoted as a new sector case.
reuse_reason = source_loop11_case_reused_for_new_R13_cross_archetype_high_MAE_4B_4C_redteam
independent_evidence_weight = 0.5 for representative rows
independent_evidence_weight = 0.25 for overlay rows
same_archetype_research = allowed
schema_rematerialization_only = false, because the trigger family is a new R13 cross-archetype guardrail test
```

## 4. Stock-Web OHLC Input / Price Source Validation

```text
source_name = FinanceData/marcap
source_repo_url = https://github.com/FinanceData/marcap
price_adjustment_status = raw_unadjusted_marcap
min_date = 1995-05-02
max_date = 2026-02-20
tradable_row_count = 14354401
raw_row_count = 15214118
symbol_count = 5414
active_like_symbol_count = 2868
inactive_or_delisted_like_symbol_count = 2546
markets = KONEX | KOSDAQ | KOSDAQ GLOBAL | KOSPI
calibration_shard_root = atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year
raw_shard_root = atlas/ohlcv_raw_by_symbol_year
schema_path = atlas/schema.json
universe_path = atlas/universe/all_symbols.csv
price_basis = tradable_raw
```

Schema confirmation:

```text
tradable_shard_columns = d,o,h,l,c,v,a,mc,s,m
raw_shard_columns = d,o,h,l,c,v,a,mc,s,m,rs
MFE_N_pct = (max high from entry_date through N tradable rows / entry_price - 1) * 100
MAE_N_pct = (min low from entry_date through N tradable rows / entry_price - 1) * 100
calibration_usable requires entry row, 180 forward tradable days, positive OHLCV, computed 30/90/180D MFE/MAE, and clean 180D corporate-action window
```

The selected R13 rows reuse source-loop stock-web calculations from loop 11. Rows that were not calibration-usable in their source files are excluded from this R13 quantitative aggregate.

## 5. Historical Eligibility Gate

All representative R13 rows satisfy:

```text
historical_event = true
entry_date_in_stock_web_tradable_shard = true
forward_180D_available = true
MFE_30D / MFE_90D / MFE_180D computed = true
MAE_30D / MAE_90D / MAE_180D computed = true
corporate_action_window_status = clean_180D_window by source-loop validation
price_basis = tradable_raw
price_adjustment_status = raw_unadjusted_marcap
```

Representative aggregate rows: **12**. Overlay-only rows: **8**. Narrative-only rows: none.

## 6. Canonical Archetype Compression Map

| R13 residual pattern | Source archetype examples | Compression logic |
|---|---|---|
| High-MAE false positive without non-price bridge | C03, C08, C17, C26, C29, C30, C31, C32 | A price move is a siren; it is not the fire report. If MAE is large and the non-price bridge is weak, cap positive-stage promotion. |
| Price-only Green false positive | C08, C17, C20, C23 | Green cannot be earned by the chart after the fact. It needs revision / margin / customer / regulatory proof at trigger date. |
| Local 4B vs full-window 4B split | C05/C20/C21/C23/C29/C32 overlays | Local peak without non-price deterioration is a watch flag. Full 4B needs valuation, legal, financing, margin, positioning, or explicit event cap evidence. |
| Hard 4C thesis break | C14, C23, C26, C29, C32 | Confirmed demand break, regulatory rejection, platform regulation, sale collapse, or thesis evidence break should route to 4C before the price fully punishes it. |
| Positive bridge preservation | C20, C21, C23, C32 | The guardrail must not punish clean structural positives: direct commercialization, capital return, global reorder, and cash tender anchor remain promotable. |

Aggregate snapshot:

```text
representative_trigger_count = 12
positive_case_count = 4
counterexample_count = 8
current_profile_error_count = 12
avg_MFE_90D_pct = 49.76
avg_MAE_90D_pct = -17.93
avg_MFE_180D_pct = 53.16
avg_MAE_180D_pct = -26.48
positive_avg_MFE_90D_pct = 120.14
positive_avg_MAE_90D_pct = -3.54
counterexample_avg_MFE_90D_pct = 14.57
counterexample_avg_MAE_90D_pct = -25.13
```

The positive group has much better return alignment than the counterexample group. The counterexample group still often has some MFE; that is exactly why the guardrail cannot be a simple “did price move?” rule. It needs the bridge: order, margin, regulatory approval, customer conversion, financing close, cash tender anchor, or comparable non-price evidence.

## 8. Positive vs Counterexample Balance

```text
positive_structural_or_bridge_cases = 4
counterexample_or_failed_rerating_cases = 8
4B_overlay_rows = 5
4C_overlay_or_trigger_rows = 4
minimum_positive_case_count = pass
minimum_counterexample_count = pass
minimum_calibration_usable_case_count = pass
```

The balance is intentionally counterexample-heavy because R13 is a red-team checkpoint. However, the four positive controls prevent the guard from becoming a blunt hammer. A good guardrail works like a circuit breaker: it trips when the current is dangerous, but it does not shut the whole building down.

## 9. Evidence Source Map

The evidence fields are inherited from the source loop 11 trigger rows. R13 does not invent new trigger-date evidence. It compresses those evidence families into cross-archetype guardrails:

```text
stage2_evidence families tested = public_event_or_disclosure, customer_or_order_quality, relative_strength, capacity_or_volume_route, policy_or_regulatory_optionality, backlog_or_delivery_visibility, early_revision_signal
stage3_evidence families tested = confirmed_revision, margin_bridge, multiple_public_sources, financial_visibility, repeat_order_or_conversion, durable_customer_confirmation, low_red_team_risk
stage4b_evidence families tested = valuation_blowoff, positioning_overheat, dilution_or_cb, capital_raise_or_overhang, legal_or_regulatory_block, margin_or_backlog_slowdown, explicit_event_cap, price_only_local_peak
stage4c_evidence families tested = contract_cancelled, call_off_or_order_cut, qualification_failure, safety_or_trial_failure, regulatory_rejection, accounting_or_trust_break, forced_liquidation_or_crash, thesis_evidence_broken
```

The source-loop trigger rows keep their original `price_shard_path` and `profile_path`. R13 rewrites only the round/canonical wrapper, not the stock-web price basis.

## 12. Trigger-Level OHLC Backtest Tables

The R13 representative rows show a familiar split:

- Structural positives can have strong MFE and tolerable MAE when a non-price bridge is present.
- False positives often still show a short MFE pop, but their MAE is large or their 180D outcome is weak.
- 4C rows are not judged by upside capture. They are judged by whether a thesis-break route would have prevented remaining inside a broken setup.

|R7|L7_BIO_HEALTHCARE_MEDICAL|C23_BIO_REGULATORY_APPROVAL_COMMERCIALIZATION|000100|유한양행|positive|direct_approval_commercialization_bridge|Stage3-Green|2024-08-20|94000|77.55|-2.66|77.55|-26.28|current_profile_too_late|
|R12|L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC|C32_GOVERNANCE_CONTROL_PREMIUM_TENDER_CAP|010130|고려아연|positive|direct_cash_tender_bridge_then_4b|Stage2-Actionable|2024-09-13|666000|261.41|-1.65|261.41|-1.65|current_profile_4B_too_late|

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

The current calibrated profile is directionally better than E2R 2.0, but loop 11 still leaves three cross-archetype leaks:

```text
current_profile_false_positive_count = 7
current_profile_too_late_or_missed_count = 3
current_profile_4B_or_4C_late_count = 2
```

Stress-test conclusions:

```text
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = existing_axis_kept, but high-MAE/no-bridge cap should sit above it
stage3_yellow_total_min = existing_axis_kept, but weak-bridge Stage3-Yellow needs demotion
stage3_green_total_min = existing_axis_kept, but price-only Green remains blocked
stage3_green_revision_min = existing_axis_kept, especially for C08/C20/C23 false Greens
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = existing_axis_kept
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = existing_axis_strengthened
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = existing_axis_strengthened
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = existing_axis_strengthened
```

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

Loop 11 cross-pattern lesson:

```text
Stage2-Actionable can work when it has a bridge: direct approval, value-up capital return, platform reorder, cash tender anchor.
Stage3-Yellow is dangerous when it is only event beta or price strength.
Stage3-Green is false when it is outcome-labeled by price rather than supported by revision/margin/customer/regulatory proof at trigger date.
```

Green lateness is not the main R13 finding here. The main finding is **score-return alignment under adverse MAE**. The guard must ask: “Did the evidence justify the drawdown risk?” not merely “Did the price go up once?”

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

|src round|symbol|company|trigger_type|entry_date|entry_price|local proximity|full-window proximity|verdict|evidence_type|
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|R12|010130|고려아연|4B|2024-11-06|1230000|0.55|0.32|non_price_4B_needed_before_full_window_peak|control_premium_or_event_premium;capital_raise_or_overhang;legal_or_regulatory_block|
|R3|247540|에코프로비엠|4B-Overlay-PriceOnly-LocalPeak|2023-07-26|455000|1.0|1.0|price_only_local_peak_not_full_4B_without_non_price_evidence|price_only;valuation_blowoff;positioning_overheat|
|R5|257720|실리콘투|4B-PriceOnlyLocalPeak|2023-10-13|10240|0.94|0.11|price_only_local_4B_too_early|price_only;positioning_overheat|
|R6|105560|KB금융|4B-PriceOnlyLocalPeak|2024-03-14|78600|1.0|0.15|price_only_local_4B_too_early|price_only;valuation_blowoff;positioning_overheat|
|R7|000100|유한양행|4B-PriceOnlyLocalPeak|2024-08-29|137100|0.84|0.59|price_only_local_4B_too_early|price_only;valuation_blowoff;positioning_overheat|

Interpretation:

```text
if local proximity high but full-window proximity low and evidence_type = price_only:
    keep as local 4B watch, not full 4B
if non-price 4B evidence exists and full-window proximity is high:
    full 4B overlay is valid
if event cap / tender cap / financing overhang exists:
    treat as explicit 4B even before final full-window peak
```

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

|src round|symbol|company|trigger_type|entry_date|entry_price|MFE90|MAE90|4C label|current verdict|
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|R1|047810|한국항공우주|4C-Watch|2023-03-14|41550|47.65|-1.32|false_break_price_only_recovery|current_profile_4C_too_late|
|R2|095340|ISC|4C-Watch|2024-08-05|42550|41.36|0.0|false_break_price_only_recovery|current_profile_4C_too_late|
|R9|018880|한온시스템|Stage4C-ThesisBreak|2023-10-13|7820|0.64|-24.94|hard_4c_success|current_profile_4C_too_late|
|R3|247540|에코프로비엠|4C-Thesis-Break-Watch|2024-04-25|234000|5.13|-30.3|hard_4c_success_if_non_price_thesis_break_confirmed|current_profile_4C_too_late|

R13 split:

```text
hard_4c_success = confirmed non-price thesis break with subsequent drawdown protection
false_break_price_only_recovery = price-only collapse followed by recovery; should be 4C-watch, not hard 4C
thesis_break_watch_only = evidence deteriorates but not yet confirmed enough for hard 4C
```

## 17. Sector-Specific Rule Candidate

```text
sector_specific_rule_candidate = false
reason = R13 is not a sector round; sector rules remain in R1~R12 files
```

R13 should not write L5/C20 or L6/C21 implementation deltas. It only passes cross-guard signals to a later batch agent.

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

```text
canonical_archetype_rule_candidate = true
canonical_scope = R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM
```

Candidate rule:

```text
IF representative trigger has weak non-price evidence bridge AND 90D/180D MAE profile is high across source loop validation,
THEN cap positive stage at Stage2-Watch or Stage2-Cap even if MFE exists.

IF price-only local peak exists WITHOUT non-price risk evidence,
THEN use 4B-watch, not full 4B.

IF non-price evidence proves thesis break,
THEN route to 4C even before the full price damage is visible.

IF non-price bridge is clean,
THEN preserve Stage2/Yellow/Green eligibility; do not let red-team guard overfit against structural positives.
```

## 19. Before / After Backtest Comparison

|profile_id|eligible_trigger_count|avg_MFE_90D_pct|avg_MAE_90D_pct|avg_MFE_180D_pct|avg_MAE_180D_pct|false_positive_rate|missed_structural_count|late_green_count|score_return_alignment_verdict|
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy|12|49.76|-17.93|53.16|-26.48|0.67|5|4|stress baseline|
|e2r_2_0_baseline_reference|12|49.76|-17.93|53.16|-26.48|0.67|5|4|stress baseline|
|r13_cross_high_MAE_guard_profile|4|120.14|-3.54|130.34|-9.44|0.0|1|3|improves false-positive filter|
|r13_4B_4C_split_guard_profile|4|120.14|-3.54|130.34|-9.44|0.0|0|3|improves false-positive filter|
|r13_counterexample_guard_profile|4|120.14|-3.54|130.34|-9.44|0.0|0|3|improves false-positive filter|

The proposed R13 profiles improve alignment not by changing historical prices, but by changing which rows would be allowed to count as positive-stage evidence. The selected positive rows retain strong MFE and tolerable MAE. The selected counterexample rows are demoted or routed to watch/4C.

## 20. Score-Return Alignment Matrix

| Alignment bucket | Source cases | R13 interpretation |
|---|---|---|
| high MFE / low-to-tolerable MAE / clean bridge | 실리콘투, KB금융, 유한양행, 고려아연 | Keep positive-stage eligibility. |
| short MFE / high MAE / weak bridge | KAI, ISC, 롯데케미칼, NAVER, 한온시스템, DL이앤씨, 한국가스공사 | Cap positive stage; watch or 4B/4C depending on evidence. |
| price-only local peak | 일부 C20/C21/C23/C29 overlays | 4B-watch only unless non-price risk exists. |
| confirmed thesis break | EV slowdown, CRL/regulatory/platform break, sale collapse | Hard 4C or 4C-watch according to evidence confirmation. |

## 23. Validation Scope / Non-Validation Scope

Validation scope:

```text
- Historical trigger-level rows from local loop 11 R1~R12 v12 MD outputs
- Stock-web price basis: tradable_raw
- Representative trigger dedupe for aggregate
- Overlay-only 4B/4C rows excluded from aggregate but included in timing audit
- Cross-archetype red-team logic only
```

Non-validation scope:

```text
- No current stock discovery
- No live candidate scan
- No brokerage/API/trading connection
- No stock_agent source code access
- No production scoring change
- No direct implementation patch
- No new price route discovery
```

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose

You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas.

These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile.

Do not blindly apply every shadow row.
Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context

- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules

- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count reused cases as new independent evidence unless independent_evidence_weight > 0.
- Do not treat schema_rematerialization_only or duplicate_low_value_loop as new evidence.
- Do not apply global deltas unless multiple large_sector_id values support the same direction.
- Prefer sector_specific or canonical_archetype_specific shadow profiles.
- Positive score promotion requires non-price evidence and clean 180D MFE/MAE.
- 4B rows are overlay/risk calibration only.
- 4C rows are thesis-break/protection calibration only.
- price-only rows cannot promote Stage2/Stage3.
- If a v12 MD weakens an already applied axis, log it as residual counterexample rather than immediately reverting.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks

1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
4. Validate novelty and reuse fields.
5. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id and reused cases.
6. Aggregate by large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
7. Update sector_shadow_profile and archetype_shadow_profile only.
8. Preserve global calibrated profile unless explicitly promoted.
9. Report new independent cases, counterexamples, and residual error types.
10. Add tests that duplicate low-value loops cannot change weights.

### R13-specific implementation caution

- R13 rows are cross-archetype guardrail rows.
- Do not map R13 rows to L5/L6/L7/L8 sector profiles.
- `R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM` should update only a red-team/checkpoint ledger unless the user explicitly asks for promotion.
- If implementing a guard, preserve positive-bridge rows and do not demote all high-MFE rows simply because some counterexamples had high MAE.

### Expected output

- Concise implementation summary.
- Rows accepted/rejected.
- New sector/canonical archetype coverage.
- Existing axis strengthened/weakened/kept.
- No investment recommendation language.
